                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Friday, May 18, 2012

                 <div class="date-posts">

                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="2034279073063739030">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     Eyuzu Japanese Cuisine, Eastin Hotel Petaling Jaya: A Weekend Shumatsu Buffet!
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2034279073063739030">
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FCFeTUC4xT8/T7VB3Y-MuII/AAAAAAAAKTQ/kdwVOl68Hko/s1600/DSC_0496.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FCFeTUC4xT8/T7VB3Y-MuII/AAAAAAAAKTQ/kdwVOl68Hko/s640/DSC_0496.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                         Drooling is allowed at Eyuzu!
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EtzIjAKYRTc/T7VBmoUZI0I/AAAAAAAAKQo/kntYKQk8U8U/s1600/DSC_0334.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EtzIjAKYRTc/T7VBmoUZI0I/AAAAAAAAKQo/kntYKQk8U8U/s640/DSC_0334.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LhzDDxdERCA/T7VBnYXiyBI/AAAAAAAAKQw/MjFqpDvMQGI/s1600/DSC_0338.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LhzDDxdERCA/T7VBnYXiyBI/AAAAAAAAKQw/MjFqpDvMQGI/s640/DSC_0338.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        A few weekends ago, a short getaway weekend at
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         <a href="http://www.eastin.com/">
                          Eastin Hotel Petaling Jaya
                         </a>
                        </b>
                        had me literally lapping up a lavish
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Shumatsu Japanese buffet
                        </b>
                        spread at
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Eyuzu Japanese
                        </b>
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Cuisine
                        </b>
                        ! No stranger to Eyuzu, as a matter of fact, this is the third time I am savoring this luscious Japanese buffet spread at Eastin. One thing for sure, each time I am back, I was treated to an even better spread than before with some additions to the spread.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SvuLpAhNoMw/T7VBoSFYlsI/AAAAAAAAKQ4/mo5SpmH3V0E/s1600/DSC_0344.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SvuLpAhNoMw/T7VBoSFYlsI/AAAAAAAAKQ4/mo5SpmH3V0E/s640/DSC_0344.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        At
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Eyuzu Japanese Cuisine
                        </b>
                        , the Shumatsu Buffet is available every Sunday for dinner only. The mecca of Japanese dishes is impeccably prepared and most the hot items are prepared fresh on the live stations. All three visits rendered excellent service and the items are refilled quickly for guests. Japanese clad kimono wait staffs are seen scurrying around to ensure guests are well served with plates cleared and drinks filled accordingly.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-UMmdG_6yvdM/T7VCFFpWjzI/AAAAAAAAKVw/YDNCfoHwfZg/s1600/DSC_0611.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-UMmdG_6yvdM/T7VCFFpWjzI/AAAAAAAAKVw/YDNCfoHwfZg/s640/DSC_0611.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        With its gorgeous min Japanese garden for a view, Eyuzu seats 130 guests including Al fresco area and private dining rooms. Featuring more than 150 mouth-watering dishes prepared by award-winning
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Japanese Executive Chef Ricky Hui
                        </b>
                        , it is indeed a luxurious treat to bring family or friends to enjoy the sumptuous buffet on the weekend.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>

                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lCggJh6F4I0/T7VB1yTlf6I/AAAAAAAAKTA/1uOGqTuu8GI/s1600/DSC_0478.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lCggJh6F4I0/T7VB1yTlf6I/AAAAAAAAKTA/1uOGqTuu8GI/s640/DSC_0478.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        My strategy to a Japanese buffet is always to check on their Sushi and Sashimi counter. A true blue Japanese meal will never be without its main superstar and the quality of the superstar should be top notch to show true authentic and quality of the buffet. Where most buffets featured a lower quality of raw fishes, Eyuzu showed otherwise with its slightly above average sashimi.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XppUlLn52sU/T7VCHgD-J5I/AAAAAAAAKWI/iyMK6dPAEsw/s1600/Sushi+Rolls.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="426" kba="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XppUlLn52sU/T7VCHgD-J5I/AAAAAAAAKWI/iyMK6dPAEsw/s640/Sushi+Rolls.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        A spread of tempting
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Sushi and Sashimi
                        </b>
                        to cater to the raw fish connoisseurs! Selections available are Salmon, Tuna, Butterfish, Snapper, Prawns and Assorted Sushi Rolls. Sashimi sliced thickly is a plus point while the sushi rolls are generously filled and coated with loads of rainbow colored flying fish roes.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qZWam690svs/T7VBqGBmBVI/AAAAAAAAKRI/7LuIs_kLq3Q/s1600/DSC_0366.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qZWam690svs/T7VBqGBmBVI/AAAAAAAAKRI/7LuIs_kLq3Q/s640/DSC_0366.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        I adored the
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Zuke Megajiki
                        </b>
                        , marinated white tuna slices bathed in a buttery and creamy garlic sauce. High praises were received from everyone around the table for this dish.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>

                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-izkgbC8gPbQ/T7VCF1hlgkI/AAAAAAAAKV4/X9EuF3Gc7WE/s1600/Cold+Appetizer.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="426" kba="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-izkgbC8gPbQ/T7VCF1hlgkI/AAAAAAAAKV4/X9EuF3Gc7WE/s640/Cold+Appetizer.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Cold appetizers of Japanese delicacies like
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Marinated Baby Octopus, Marinated Hotate, Marinated Jelly Fish
                        </b>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Japanese Seaweed
                        </b>
                        is chilled on ice bars to whet appetites of the brave while
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Fried Fish Skin, Crabstick, Seaweed, Crispy Prawns
                        </b>
                        and more awaits you! My favorite is the light and crispy fish skin which resembles addictive crackers.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>

                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DAhwVdrB4uM/T7VBq3rsg5I/AAAAAAAAKRQ/YBO95t3kGNQ/s1600/DSC_0371.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DAhwVdrB4uM/T7VBq3rsg5I/AAAAAAAAKRQ/YBO95t3kGNQ/s640/DSC_0371.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                         Chilled Prawns
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Fresh Oysters
                        </b>
                        are glistening on top of crushed ice where sweet crustaceans and mollusks are enjoyed with just a squeeze of lemon. Had a few of these each time and it was thoroughly satisfying for freshness and sweetness of the sea.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qZgRMjnB55A/T7VB7u-JQrI/AAAAAAAAKUA/4l2kP2SC1ao/s640/DSC_0538.JPG" width="426"/>
                      </a>

                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GdJvwFbE3to/T7VB5ote45I/AAAAAAAAKTo/iEJ1y3iy_qc/s640/DSC_0514.JPG" width="640"/>

                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        A
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Fukahire Soup
                        </b>
                        or Sharks Fin Soup and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Chawan Mushi
                        </b>
                        cater to guest of all ages.
                       </span>
                      </span>

                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Oodles of noodles are displaying prettily coiled up where one can savored
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Chilled Soba
                        </b>
                        or
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Green Tea Soba
                        </b>
                        and slurped up thick
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Udon
                        </b>
                        in hot broth. Simplicity at its best as the noodles!

                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Hot warmers housed an array of
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Kaki Motoyaki, Dory Batayaki, Grilled Chicken Wings, Chicken Teriyaki, Grilled Unagi, Age Tofu
                        </b>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Yasai Itame
                        </b>
                        . Go straight for the creamy baked oysters and unagi for pure seafood sensation!

                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-2RcjF-AR7pE/T7VB_vmy8II/AAAAAAAAKUw/SGczj7Y6pqk/s1600/DSC_0576.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-2RcjF-AR7pE/T7VB_vmy8II/AAAAAAAAKUw/SGczj7Y6pqk/s640/DSC_0576.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Live stations like
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Teppanyaki
                        </b>
                        features a nice selection of
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Beef, Salmon, Chicken, Squid
                        </b>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Slipper Lobster
                        </b>
                        with a medley of vegetables and mushrooms. Simply select your choices and watch the chef whip up your platter of teppanyaki. I had quite a few of the Slipper Lobsters which was sweet and very delectable on the palate with just a squeeze of lemon!
                       </span>
                      </span>

                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">

                        </b>
                        for hotpots and shabu shabu,
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">

                        </b>
                        ,
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Kushiyaki Station
                        </b>
                        for grilled skewers of meat and seafood and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Katsu station
                        </b>
                        . The plethora of ingredients for all the stations will have guest spoiled for choice. Select your fancy and let the chefs do the work.

                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                         Dobin Mushi
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        , a traditional Japanese broth served in neat little ceramic teapots, holds a delicate broth coupled with seafood. A light squeeze of lime lifted up the aroma of the broth. One is asked to savor the broth poured into little tea cups before savoring the treasures in the pot.

                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                         Oyster Teppanyaki
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        was delicately wrapped in egg omelette and served in its own shell. A savory teppanyaki sauce wrapped up the briny and juicy oysters!
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-njxwEER37pY/T7VCDmLcVmI/AAAAAAAAKVg/6sZ9FnaBP-Y/s1600/DSC_0600.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-njxwEER37pY/T7VCDmLcVmI/AAAAAAAAKVg/6sZ9FnaBP-Y/s640/DSC_0600.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        A special dessert was creatively section into three desserts of
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Green Tea Mousse, Lime Ice Cream and Fruits
                        </b>
                        . Mousse was creamy and wobbly while the Lime Ice Cream was simply-out-of-this-world for me since I love sour flavors.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-coBKPETxL2g/T7VB4IH9cNI/AAAAAAAAKTY/cQ541nIpBm8/s1600/DSC_0501.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-coBKPETxL2g/T7VB4IH9cNI/AAAAAAAAKTY/cQ541nIpBm8/s640/DSC_0501.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                         Hot or Cold Sake
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        is simply a must for Japanese cuisine to round up the meal!
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DAADjAEv6ho/T7VBiO6-aFI/AAAAAAAAKP4/a3091Xaalpg/s1600/DSC_0177+%25282%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" kba="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DAADjAEv6ho/T7VBiO6-aFI/AAAAAAAAKP4/a3091Xaalpg/s640/DSC_0177+%25282%2529.JPG" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                         Eyuzu Japanese Cuisine
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                        is definitely a must for those who enjoy a selection of Japanese cuisine. As mentioned, my third visit is still a charm as the selections are plenty and quality is definitely one of the better ones around the city.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif";'>
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Available for dinner only, the buffet is served every Sunday from 6.30pm to 10.00pm, at RM86.00++ for adults and RM43.00++ for child. For reservations and enquiries, please call 603  7665 1111 extension 203.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>

                         EYUZU JAPANESE CUISINE
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">

                       <span style='font-family: "Verdana", "sans-serif"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>

      var config = {'blogId': '2153116117081957032', 'postId': '2034279073063739030', 'feed': 'http://www.chasingfooddreams.com/feeds/2034279073063739030/comments/default', 'authorName': 'Chasing Food Dreams CFD', 'authorUrl': 'https://www.blogger.com/profile/15654596657978881855', 'baseUri': 'https://www.blogger.com', 'maxThreadDepth': 2};

      var cursor = null;
      if (items &amp;&amp; items.length &gt; 0) {
        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
      }

      var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '&lt;span class="deleted-comment"&gt;' + entry.content.$t + '&lt;/span&gt;';
            }
          }
        }
        return entry.content.$t;
      }

      var parse = function(data) {
        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];
        if (data &amp;&amp; data.feed &amp;&amp; data.feed.entry) {
          for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author &amp;&amp; entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {
                comment.author = {
                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };
              }
            }
            if (entry.link) {
              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid &amp;&amp; pid[1]) {
                  comment.parentId = pid[1];
                }
              }
            }
            comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
              for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                  comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                  comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                }
              }
            }
            comments.push(comment);
          }
        }
        return comments;
      };

      var paginator = function(callback) {
        if (hasMore()) {
          var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&amp;v=2&amp;orderby=published&amp;reverse=false&amp;max-results=50';
          if (cursor) {
            url += '&amp;published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
          }
          window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
            var parsed = parse(data);
            cursor = parsed.length &lt; 50 ? null
                : parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
            callback(parsed);
            window.bloggercomments = null;
          }
          url += '&amp;callback=bloggercomments';
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = 'text/javascript';
          script.src = url;
          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
      };
      var hasMore = function() {
        return !!cursor;
      };
      var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
        if ('iswriter' == key) {
          var matches = !!comment.author
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.name == config.authorName
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
          return matches ? 'true' : '';
        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
          return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID='
               + config.blogId + '&amp;postID=' + comment.id;
        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
          return comment.deleteclass;
        }
        return '';
      };

      var replybox = null;
      var replyUrlParts = null;
      var replyParent = undefined;

      var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
        if (replybox == null) {
          // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
          replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
          if (replybox != null) {
            replybox.height = '250px';
            replybox.style.display = 'block';
            replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
          }
        }
        if (replybox &amp;&amp; (commentId !== replyParent)) {
          document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(replybox, null);
          replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0]
              + (commentId ? '&amp;parentID=' + commentId : '')
              + '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
          replyParent = commentId;
        }
      };

      var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
      var startThread, targetComment;
      if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
      } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
      }

      // Configure commenting API:
      var configJso = {
        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
      };
      var provider = {
        'id': config.postId,
        'data': items,
        'loadNext': paginator,
        'hasMore': hasMore,
        'getMeta': getMeta,
        'onReply': onReply,
        'rendered': true,
        'initComment': targetComment,
        'initReplyThread': startThread,
        'config': configJso,
        'messages': msgs
      };

      var render = function() {
        if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
          var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
          window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
        }
      };

      // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
      if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
        render();
      } else {
        window.goog = window.goog || {};
        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);

                <h2 class="title">
                 About Me
                </h2>
                <div class="widget-content">
                 Life is about the chase.. chasing after your dreams, chasing after your loves and chasing after your passion. So here's my journal on my chase for my dreams.
                 <div>
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                  Be Different, be Yourself!
                 </div>

    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
